package LessLeavesRec;
public class LessLeavesRec {
    public static Tree append(Tree x, Tree y) {
                // adds y to the right bottom of x
                if (x == null) return y;
                else return new Tree(x.l, append(x.r,y));
    }

    // checks whether one tree has less leaves than the other
    public static boolean lessleaves(Tree x, Tree y){
                if (y == null) {
                        return false;
                } else {
                        if (x == null) {
                                return true;
                        } else {
                                return lessleaves(append(x.l,x.r), append(y.l,y.r));
                        }
            }
        }

        public static void main(String[] args) {
                Random.args = args;
                Tree x = Tree.createTree();
                Tree y = Tree.createTree();
          
                boolean b = lessleaves(x,y);
        }
}


package LessLeavesRec;
public class Random {
    static String[] args;
    static int index = 0;

    public static int random() {
        if (args.length <= index) {
            return 0;
        }
        final String string = args[index];
        index++;
        if (string == null) {
            return 0;
        }
        return string.length();
    }
}


package LessLeavesRec;

public class Tree {
    Tree l;
    Tree r;
    int value;

    public Tree(final Tree l, final Tree r) {
        this.l = l;
        this.r = r;
    }

    public Tree() {
    }

    public static Tree createNode() {
        final Tree result = new Tree();
        result.value = Random.random();
        return result;
    }




   public static Tree createTree() {
        int counter = Random.random();
        if (counter == 0) {
            return null;
        }
        final Tree result = createNode();
        Tree t = result;

        while (counter > 0) {
            final int branch = Random.random();
            if (branch > 0) {
                if (t.l == null) {
                    t.l = createNode();
                    t = result;
                } else {
                    t = t.l;
                }
            } else {
                if (t.r == null) {
                    t.r = createNode();
                    t = result;
                } else {
                    t = t.r;
                }
            }
            counter--;
        }

        return result;
    }
}

public class LessLeavesRec {
    public static Tree append(Tree x, Tree y) {
                // adds y to the right bottom of x

public class Random {
    static String[] args;
    static int index = 0;

    public static int random() {
        if (args.length <= index) {
            return 0;
        }
        final String string = args[index];
        index++;

            return 0;
        }
        return string.length();

package LessLeavesRec;

public class Tree {
    Tree l;
    Tree r;
    int value;

    public Tree(final Tree l, final Tree r) {
        this.l = l;
        this.r = r;
    }

    public Tree() {
    }

    public static Tree createNode() {
        final Tree result = new Tree();
        result.value = Random.random();
        return result;
    }




   public static Tree createTree() {
        int counter = Random.random();
        if (counter == 0) {
            return null;
        }
        final Tree result = createNode();
        Tree t = result;

        while (counter > 0) {
            final int branch = Random.random();
            if (branch > 0) {
                if (t.l == null) {
                    t.l = createNode();
                    t = result;
                } else {
                    t = t.l;
                }
            } else {
                if (t.r == null) {
                    t.r = createNode();
                    t = result;
                } else {
                    t = t.r;
                }
            }
            counter--;
        }

        return result;
    }
}
